                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">所有的</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">单纯</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">龋病</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">都没有牙龈的损害，因此，</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">临床表现逐渐接近可复性牙髓炎</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">【无自发痛，有冷热刺激一过性痛等】</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">，但温度</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">测试</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">等无反应</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">。</span>
                        </p>

                    <td style="width:23.8%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">可以理解成可探牙髓萎缩，因而不常受刺激，不呈现自发痛，但一旦刺激同急性牙髓炎。因此</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">浅探不痛，深探痛</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td style="width:28.18%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                            <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">增生性牙髓炎</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">青少年</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:Cambria">&#xa0;</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:23.8%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">肉芽组织增生，无神经浸润到肉芽组织中，所以探诊不痛；而肉芽组织中有大量毛细血管，</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">极易出血</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td style="width:28.18%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">残髓炎</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:Cambria">&#xa0;</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:Cambria">&#xa0;</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:23.8%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">常常发生在根尖孔，所以常有叩痛和咬合痛（同根尖周病）</span>
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">自发钝痛，</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">放射性痛和温度刺激痛</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>

                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">先引起根尖炎症，然后向冠方蔓延</span>
                        </p>

                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">长期牙周炎突有牙髓炎症状（其他的牙髓病变大多是龋源性）</span>

            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:26pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">&#xa0;</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:26pt">
                <br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both"/>
            </p>
            <h1 style="margin-top:17pt; margin-bottom:16.5pt; text-align:justify; page-break-inside:avoid; page-break-after:avoid; line-height:241%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:22pt">
                <span style="font-family:'等线'">口腔外科学</span>
            </h1>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:14pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">临床麻醉</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">（局部麻醉）</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">（一）、麻醉药物</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">利多卡因：最常用，适用于有心律失常的人；</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">普鲁卡因：毒性最小，但是免疫原性最强；</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">丁卡因：渗透性好，但是毒性强。</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">（二）、</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">麻醉方法</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">1</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">．表面麻醉</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">（</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">1%</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">丁卡因，</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">1~2%</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">利多卡因）</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">；</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">2</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">．浸润麻醉（</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">1~2%</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">利多卡因）</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">：</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">皮丘注射法；</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">骨膜上浸润法（适合</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">上、下颌牙槽突前份相关部位，原因是这些部分骨质疏松</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">）；</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">牙周膜注射法（疼，但是适合容易出血的患者）。</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">3</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">．</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">1)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">上颌神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">翼腭管注射法：标志为腭大孔</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">（</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">上颌第三或第二磨牙腭侧龈缘至腭中线的中外</span>
                    <span style="font-weight:bold">1/3</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">处</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">）</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">口外注射法：标志为颧弓及下颌切迹。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">2)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">上牙槽后神经阻滞麻醉</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">【翼静脉丛，血肿】</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">进针点：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">上颌第二磨牙远中颊侧的口腔前庭沟</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">麻醉范围：麻醉范围包括除上颌第一磨牙颊侧近中根外的同侧上颌磨牙、牙槽突及相应的颊侧软组织。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">3)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">眶下神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">口外注射法</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:126pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'">进针点：自同侧鼻翼旁约</span>
                <span style="font-family:Cambria">1cm</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span>
            </p>
            <ol start="2" type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">口内注射法</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:126pt; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'">进针点：上颌侧切牙口腔前庭沟处。</span>
            </p>
            <ol start="3" type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.06pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.94pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">麻醉范围：同侧下睑、鼻、眶下区、上唇、上颌前牙、前磨牙以及这些牙唇侧或颊侧的牙槽突、骨膜、牙龈和黏膜等组织。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">4)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">腭前神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">适应症：上颌前磨牙与磨牙拔除术的腭侧麻醉、腭隆突切除及腭裂整复术等。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">进针点：同上颌神经阻滞麻醉翼腭管注射法。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.06pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.94pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">麻醉范围包括同侧磨牙、前磨牙腭侧的黏骨膜、牙龈及牙槽突等。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">5)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">鼻腭神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">适应症：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌前牙拔除及颌骨囊肿剜除等手术的腭侧麻醉。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">进针点：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭前孔</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">（切牙孔）</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.06pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.94pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">麻醉范围：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">两侧尖牙连线前方的腭侧牙龈、黏骨膜和牙槽突。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">6)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">下颌神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">适应症：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">范围较广的下颌骨手术及三叉神经第三支痛的诊断与鉴别诊断。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:98.27pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:6.73pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt; font-weight:bold">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">进针点：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:normal">颧弓及下颌切迹。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.06pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.94pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">麻醉范围：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">同侧下颌牙舌前</span>
                    <span>2/3</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">、口底、下颌骨及颌周组织、升颌肌群、颞部皮肤及颊部皮肤黏膜等。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">7)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">下牙槽神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:98.28pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:6.72pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt; font-weight:bold">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">进针点：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:normal">翼下颌皱襞中点外侧</span>
                    <span style="font-weight:normal">0.3~0.4cm</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:normal">或颊脂垫尖。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">麻醉范围：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">同侧下颌骨、下颌牙、牙周膜、前磨牙至中切牙的唇颊侧牙龈黏骨膜和下唇。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">8)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">舌神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">进针点：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">下牙槽神经前内</span>
                    <span>1cm</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">处。因此，在进行下牙槽神经阻滞注射后，将注射针退出</span>
                    <span>1cm</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">，再注射麻药</span>
                    <span>1ml</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">，或边退边注射麻药，即可麻醉舌神经。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">麻醉范围：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">同侧舌前</span>
                    <span>2/3</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">、下颌舌侧牙龈、黏骨膜及口底黏膜。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:84pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-21pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                <span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold">9)</span>
                <span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;</span>
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">颊神经阻滞麻醉</span>
            </p>
            <ol type="A" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt">
                <li style="margin-left:97.7pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.3pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">进针点：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">在行下牙槽神经和舌神经阻滞麻醉后，将针尖退至肌层黏膜下，注射麻药</span>
                    <span>1ml</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">，即可麻醉颊神经。</span>
                </li>
                <li style="margin-left:97.57pt; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:7.43pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt">
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">麻醉范围：</span>
                    <span style="font-family:'宋体'">下颌磨牙颊侧牙龈、黏骨膜颊部黏膜、肌肉和皮肤。</span>
                </li>
            </ol>
            <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; line-height:150%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:14pt">
                <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">口腔颌面部肿瘤</span>
            </p>
            <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="width:100%; border-collapse:collapse">
                <tr>
                    <td style="width:28.18%; border-bottom:0.75pt solid #c9c9c9; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:center; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:11pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">疾病</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; border-bottom:0.75pt solid #c9c9c9; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:center; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:11pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">组织学起源</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; border-bottom:0.75pt solid #c9c9c9; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:center; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:11pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">好发</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">人群和</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">部位</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:23.78%; border-bottom:0.75pt solid #c9c9c9; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:center; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:11pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">备注</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td colspan="4" style="padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:14pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">软组织囊肿</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">（不含唾液腺）</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td style="width:28.18%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">皮脂腺囊肿</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">（粉瘤）</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">非真性肿瘤</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:Cambria">&#xa0;</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:23.78%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">特征：中间一个</span>
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">色素点</span>
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">手术梭形切口</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td style="width:28.18%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">皮样和表皮样囊肿</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">胚胎发育遗留在组织中的上皮细胞或手术的意外种植</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:24.02%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">儿童和青年</span>
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">前者好发于口底和颏下区；后者好发于口裂以上</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:23.78%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top; background-color:#ededed">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">腐败色豆腐渣样分泌物</span>
                        </p>

                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">腭部小唾液腺</span>
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">腮腺</span>
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">舌下腺发生极少，但舌下腺的肿瘤基本都是腺样囊性癌</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                    <td style="width:23.78%; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top">
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">血管和神经侵犯</span>
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt">
                            <span style="font-family:'宋体'">淋巴结很少转移</span>
                        </p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
